<div id="a216" style="position:absolute;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:16px;left:404px;top:990px;">2</div><div id="a218" style="position:absolute;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:16px;left:310px;top:67px;">THE CATO<div style="display:inline-block;width:6px">&#160;</div>CORPORATION<div style="display:inline-block;width:6px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a225" style="position:absolute;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-weight:bold;left:96px;top:105px;">Item 2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition</div><div id="a228" style="position:absolute;font-family:'Times New Roman';left:96px;top:139px;">On November 21, 2024 The Cato Corporation issued a press Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:460.4px;">share, compared to net loss of $0.5 million or ($0.02) per diluted share<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.34px">&#160;</div>for the nine months ended October 28, 2023.<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.41px">&#160;</div>Sales </div><div id="a55" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:477.2px;">for the nine months ended November 2, 2024 were $486.8 million,<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.32px">&#160;</div>a decrease of 8% to sales of $528.2 million for the </div><div id="a57" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:494px;">nine months ended October 28, 2023.<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.83px">&#160;</div>Year-to-date same-store sales decreased 4% compared to 2023. </div><div id="a66" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:527.76px;">&#8220;Our third quarter sales trend deteriorated from second quarter, in part due to three major hurricanes over<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.23px">&#160;</div>a five week </div><div id="a68" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:547.14px;">span, supply chain issues causing late merchandise receipts to the stores<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.33px">&#160;</div>and continued negative pressure on our </div><div id="a69" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:566.66px;">customers&#8217; disposable income,&#8221; stated John Cato, Chairman,<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.3px">&#160;</div>President, and Chief Executive Officer.<div style="display:inline-block;width:7.89px">&#160;</div>&#8220;We are managing </div><div id="a71" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:586.02px;">both SG&amp;A expenses and inventory levels in line with our current<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.32px">&#160;</div>sales trend.<div style="display:inline-block;width:7.22px">&#160;</div>However, we continue to incur higher </div><div id="a72" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:605.38px;">costs to move inventory to our stores due to the bankruptcy of a carrier<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.32px">&#160;</div>that previously serviced 50% of our stores, as well </div><div id="a74" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:624.74px;">as, higher distribution costs associated with conversion issues for a distribution<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.18px">&#160;</div>center systems and automation upgrade.<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.54px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a75" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:644.1px;">We believe that the fourth quarter will remain challenging.&#8221; </div><div id="a78" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:680.42px;">Gross margin decreased from 32.5% to 28.8% of sales in the quarter due to higher<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.2px">&#160;</div>markdowns, as well as, increased </div><div id="a79" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:697.38px;">freight, distribution and occupancy costs as a percent of sales.<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.03px">&#160;</div>SG&amp;A expenses as a percent of sales increased from </div><div id="a81" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:714.18px;">39.4% to 40.0% of sales during the quarter primarily due to deleveraging<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.2px">&#160;</div>of payroll costs, partially offset by lower </div><div id="a82" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:730.98px;">advertising and insurance expenses.<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.68px">&#160;</div>SG&amp;A expenses were $3.9 million lower than last year due<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.24px">&#160;</div>to lower payroll, </div><div id="a83" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:747.94px;">advertising and insurance costs. Tax expense for the quarter was $0.3 million versus a tax benefit of $4.3 million in<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.3px">&#160;</div>the </div><div id="a85" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:764.74px;">prior year, primarily due to valuation allowances against net deferred tax assets. </div><div id="a88" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:798.54px;">Year<div style="display:inline-block;width:1.46px">&#160;</div>-to-date gross margin decreased to 33.3% of sales from 34.6% in the prior year primarily<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.04px">&#160;</div>due to increased occupancy, </div><div id="a93" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:817.9px;">freight and distribution costs as a percent of sales, partially offset by increased merchandise<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.15px">&#160;</div>margins.<div style="display:inline-block;width:7.24px">&#160;</div>The year-to-date </div><div id="a98" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:837.26px;">SG&amp;A rate was 35.5% versus 35.1% primarily due to deleveraging<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.28px">&#160;</div>of payroll costs and insurance costs, partially offset by </div><div id="a101" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:856.78px;">lower advertising costs.<div style="display:inline-block;width:7px">&#160;</div>SG&amp;A expenses were $12.5 million lower than last year due to lower<div style="display:inline-block;width:2.33px">&#160;</div>payroll, insurance and </div><div id="a103" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:876.14px;">advertising costs. Tax expense for the nine-month period was $1.6 million compared to $0.8 million tax benefit last year, </div><div id="a107" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Times New Roman&apos;;font-size:14.72px;left:48px;top:895.5px;">primarily due to valuation allowances against net deferred tax assets. </div></div>

/* styles for footnote marker */
..report .fn {
	white-space: nowrap;
}

	text-align: right;
	white-space: nowrap;
}

	padding-left: 2em;
}

	padding: 0px 0.4em 0px 2em;
}

	text-align: left;
	white-space: normal;
}

	margin-bottom: 1em;
	width: 17em;
}

	display: none;
}

	font-weight: bold;
}

}
